# Shadow Priest auras

## 1. Insanity bar

A bar containing the current insanity, with dropdown rate, haste%, stacks of Voidform.

![Example image](insanity-bar.jpg)

## 2. Auspicious spirits tracker

Tracks the number of Auspicious spirits and the amount of insanity they will give.

![Example image](auspicious-spirits.jpg)

## 3. Voidform tracker

Tracks the number of stacks of voidform

![Example image](voidform-stacks.jpg)

## 4. Cooldowns bar

Tracks the cooldowns of the main dps cooldowns.

![Example image](cd-bar.jpg)

## 5. DoT tracking and spell bar

Tracks the principal shadow priest spells.

![Example image](spells-bar.jpg)

## 6. Weak Aura import strings

## 6.1 Insanity bar
